<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehoor.html>gehoor</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghehoor</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghehoer</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Gehöör</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gehör</i>.
</p>

***gehorig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gehorig.html>gehorig</a> (83326)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">horig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehorig.html>gehorig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gehoriger</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gehorigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Middle Ages</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> being in a serf-like relationship to a lord</li>
<li>obedient</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehoor.html>gehoor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hearing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehorig.html>gehorig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gehoriger</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gehorigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>being easy to hear the noises in the neighbouring <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a> or buildings; noisy, thin-walled</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slechte.html>slechte</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:functioneren.html>functioneren</a> geluidsisolatie <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluiden.html>geluiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamers.html>kamers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a>

***gehucht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gehucht.html>gehucht</a> (25369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghehochte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghehuchte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gihufti</i>. Ultimately a combination of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gehöft</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> perhaps of Dutch origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehucht.html>gehucht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehuchten.html>gehuchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehuchtje.html>gehuchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a>; a tiny settlement, often without a church
<ul><li><b>1637</b> January 19, Pieter Corneliszoon <a href = vnd.unilang:hooft.html>Hooft</a>, "861 Aen <a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>Zijne</a> Hooghejt", in H.W <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Tricht (ed.), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> briefwisseling <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> P.C. <a href = vnd.unilang:hooft.html>Hooft</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 2, Tjeenk Willink (publ., 1977), page 914, lines 5 to 8.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Bijlmer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gehucht.html>gehucht</a></b> oft gebujrte behoorende, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> lidt <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Weesperkerspel, <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Castelajnschap <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Mujden ende Baljuwschap <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Goejlandt, ende paelende aen <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a> Meerken genaemt <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Bijlmermeer.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> The Bijlmer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a></b> or small community belonging, as a member of Weesperkerspel, under the castellany of Muiden and the bailiwick of Gooiland, and bordering on a certain small lake called the Bijlmermeer.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlek.html>vlek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gheil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:geil.html>geil</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:gail.html>gail</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gailaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰoylos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">frothing, tempestuous, wanton</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***geit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geit.html>geit</a> (5554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geit.html>geit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:geit.html>geit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaits</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stratum_(linguistics)" class="extiw" title="w:Stratum (linguistics)">substrate</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geit.html>geit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geiten.html>geiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geitje.html>geitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>goat, any member of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:capra.html>Capra</a></i></li>
<li>goat (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:capra.html>Capra</a> aegagrus</i>) or the domesticated goat (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:capra.html>Capra</a> aegagrus hircus</i>)</li>
<li>Any female of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:capra.html>Capra</a></i> or of the above (sub)species.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a> (219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geck</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">madman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Earlier origin unknown, possibly dialectal and/or from unknown substrate; however, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Geck</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Jeck</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">geek</i> (see etymology there).
